It was mainly because it was close to the Henan Museum we were going to (it turned out not to be close, haha), and it was relatively cost-effective. The hotel lobby, cafe and restaurant are under a huge dome, which was quite shocking at first sight. I wanted to sit there and drink a cup of coffee or be in a daze. The check-in at the front desk was quick and professional, and the waiter also greeted me politely. The room is relatively small, but I like the simple French style. There are welcome fruits, bedding and toiletries are good, especially the bamboo toothbrush and paper-wrapped toothpaste, which are very environmentally friendly. This is the first time I have seen it in a hotel I have stayed in, and I am impressed. At night, I made the bed, and the bathroom and the bed were covered with foot pad towels, a total of four pieces. I met the manager and told him my thoughts. I felt that this was a bit wasteful and not environmentally friendly. The manager was very nice and said that he would report these opinions. The hotel's breakfast is very rich, the ingredients are fresh, and the foreman and waiter are very polite, thoughtful and professional. In short, I was very satisfied with this stay.

msg:The surrounding environment is very good. Although it is close to the main road, it is not noisy at all. There are abundant green plants and flowers. There is a gym and a swimming pool. Zijingshan Park is across the street, which is quite suitable for vacation. It is only three or four kilometers to go to People's Park to enjoy flowers and visit the museum.
The room is quite spacious, the lighting is relatively warm, and the sanitation is in place. Towels and bedding are very useful. The mattress is a bit soft for me.
The waiter is warm and polite. The concierge takes the initiative to greet and help with luggage. Meow Meow, Zhenzhen, and Tingli, who are on duty at the front desk, provide very standardized services and give patient and clear instructions.
The breakfast has a wide variety of flavors, and there is no lack of local specialties such as spicy soup and sha soup.
Overall, it is very good, so I stayed longer.
The kettle is still old-fashioned, and the shell is not insulated. I was accidentally scalded. The trash can in the bathroom is not practical. There are no hooks to hang clothes or towels in the bathroom of the swimming pool, and there are no cotton swabs on the dressing table. If it can be improved, the check-in experience will be better.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted April 17, 2024
msg:Feel at home: the wonderful experience of Sofitel Zhengzhou International Hotel

Staying at Sofitel Zhengzhou International Hotel is like stepping into a quiet paradise. This hotel is located in the center of the bustling city, but it can make people feel at home away from the hustle and bustle.
The hotel's environment is unique, the architectural design is simple and generous, and it combines modern and traditional elements, which is refreshing. Walking in the hotel, you can see carefully crafted garden landscapes everywhere, which makes people feel happy and relaxed.
The superior geographical location is a highlight of the hotel. It is located in the center of Zhengzhou, with convenient transportation, allowing you to easily reach major business districts, tourist attractions and transportation hubs. This convenient location provides great convenience for your travel. Every morning, when I walked into the hotel's restaurant, I was attracted by the exquisite breakfast. The rich and diverse dishes all show the chefs' care and professionalism. Whether it is Western or Chinese, every dish makes people appetizing and injects vitality and beauty into the new day.
And the guest rooms are even more unforgettable. The spacious and bright space and the comfortable and soft beds make people find the warm feeling of home during the tiring journey. The facilities in the room are complete, and every detail reflects the hotel's pursuit of guest comfort.
However, what I remember most are the three customer service managers at the hotel front desk: Miaomiao, Lili, and Zenghui. With their beautiful and generous smiles and friendly hospitality, they made me feel like reuniting with my family. Whether it was the polite greetings when checking in or the patient answers when I encountered problems, they provided me with meticulous service with the most sincere attitude, which made me feel warm and moved.
In summary, Sofitel International Zhengzhou is undoubtedly a place to live that people yearn for. The beautiful environment, convenient geographical location, exquisite breakfast, comfortable rooms, and warm and thoughtful service all make people feel at home. I sincerely thank the hotel for everything it has provided and look forward to visiting again.

What impressed me more was the service here. After I checked out, I asked the staff in the lobby for help because I needed to handle some affairs first and it was inconvenient to carry a suitcase. Meow Meow, this enthusiastic staff member, took the initiative to add my WeChat after learning about my needs, and promised to personally follow up on my luggage storage. Her move made my originally anxious mood instantly relieved a lot.
When confirming the mailing matters, Meow Meow quickly placed the mailing order and took a photo to send it to me for confirmation. The whole service process was professional, enthusiastic and efficient. In contrast, I accidentally left my belongings after checking out of another newly opened hotel in Zhengzhou. However, the service of that hotel disappointed me. After a day and a night, no one contacted me to remind me that I had left my belongings. I was ready to give up, but after Miaomiao learned about it, she immediately contacted the other hotel and successfully connected my belongings to me. This kind of thoughtful and considerate service touched me deeply.
This stay in this five-star hotel made me deeply understand what is the real quality service. Whether it is the decoration of the lobby, the design of the dome, or the warm and thoughtful service of the staff, it shows the unique charm of this hotel. Here, I feel the warmth and comfort of home, and also experience the noble enjoyment of being at home.
Therefore, I have no hesitation in giving this five-star hotel a five-star rating. I believe that whether it is a business trip or a leisure vacation, this place will be an ideal choice. Looking forward to the next stay, looking forward to feeling the warmth and beauty here again!
